### Quora -  Astrological Question and Answers by Steve Hora
{{< rawhtml >}}
<div><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What does your ascendant mean?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In a day, from sunrise till next sunrise, the earth rotates on itself. As it rotates, a place on Earth e.g. Mumbai, will rotate through the whole zodiac of Aries till Pisces.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For a given birth, the sign and degree in which Sun rises, gives Sun position (minus ayanamsa). From that position, the ascendant is calculated based on that many hours-minutes, elapsed. Roughly it is 2 hours for each sign.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Another way is - The zodiac degree at which the horizon is at the time of event or birth minus ayanamsa is Ascendant.</p><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In Nadi palm leaf readings, the ascendant or lagna degree is called as &#8220;Uyir&#8221; in Tamil, meaning Life breath or Prana.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#8220;Mei&#8221; in tamil, meaning Body, is lagna house,</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Uyir-Mei is living body. And Tamil alphabets are called UyirMei letters.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Chandra is called as &#8220;Mathi&#8221; in tamil, meaning Intelligence and Emotions.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">And the proverb in Tamil is &#8220;Vidhi-ai Mathi-yal Vellalam&#8221;, One can win over Fate with Intelligence or Free will. There is a way to remedy bad karma using Chandra, astrologically.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Long live Tamil and Blessed are Tamilians.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So be it. Tathastu.</p></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">My obeisance to Tamil Sage and SapthaRishi Agasthya.</p><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-eab87739d56eb8cf6316c4471d8ddf6e" master_src="/img/qimg-eab87739d56eb8cf6316c4471d8ddf6e" master_w="275" master_h="183" /></div></div></blockquote></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Sep 24, 2019 07:00 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What are the meanings of different houses in a D10 chart?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/profile/Sheshachalam-Iyengar">Sheshachalam Iyengar</a></span> in his answer has explained it.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Houses or signs and bhava or rashi chart in terms of divisional charts to be considered, to mathematically derive any.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Considering D10 as a chart by itself, begs explanation, for any graha placement, or lordship or power (neecha or oucha).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">At least D9 has a proper definition in terms of nakshatra padas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Going by above considerations, all other divisional charts have this definition as told, with its stated anomalies.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-80c3b4700015c6dc01792ad10928ddc3" master_src="/img/qimg-80c3b4700015c6dc01792ad10928ddc3" master_w="193" master_h="130" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">A closer look at D60 reveals secrets from a Nadi perspective. The same analogy can be used to derive mathematically, deduce and predict any divisional charts.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">D150 becomes more difficult and becomes mysterious, and looks like one has to acquire and use divine powers, to predict.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Sep 26, 2019 09:21 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the scientific basis of Nadi palm leaf astrology to predict accurately?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/What-is-the-scientific-basis-of-Nadi-palm-leaf-astrology-to-predict-accurately/answers/93995110">Steve Hora's answer to What is the scientific basis of Nadi palm leaf astrology to predict accurately?</a></span></p></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Refer above question&#8217;s answer.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Further research into Nadi Palm leaf timing methodology is as below.</p><ol><li>It does NOT follow Vimshottari Dasha system.</li><li>It does NOT use Chandra as the base for timing.</li><li>It uses all divisional charts, for prediction of event.</li><li>The timing of event is by Navamsa, D60 and D150.</li><li>The reading of a set of lines or stanzas is in multiples of 3 or 5, based on which Amsa chart is used for timing.</li><li>Mostly it is 3 years, so it is D60 being used.</li><li>Moving the house, for each set of years, gets the prediction.</li></ol><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-e60088dcedc9308239c935e1ed06c067" PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What happens when Rahu is in the 9th house in Gemini?</span></div><div><strong>Content: For sure. No.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Signs also are the same.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When anybody looks into the night sky, there is no boundaries to mark the sky as 1st house or this or that sign.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are many house system, namely UnEqual houses (Placidus) or Equal houses or more.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>All these are imaginations of a fertile mind of humans, nothing on the sky. Same goes for signs also.</b></p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-3ef825ac119b2d74adb898faed3a63b7" master_src="/img/qimg-3ef825ac119b2d74adb898faed3a63b7" master_w="326" master_h="314" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">That said, observations by the humans, brought in houses and signs into our understanding. And understandings goes, there are varied opinion among all.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Then again were the first house starts is not accepted properly by Sidereal or Tropical.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">To KISS (Keep It Simple Standard), just accept Houses and Signs are just same with a proper starting point.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Then your understanding will fall in place.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Nov 01, 2019 10:11 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the difference between sidereal and tropical astrology?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Keeping math and the analytical thing apart for both type of Astrology, below goes my thesis.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Sun is the center for our solar system. Th Solar system moves or drifts as a disk around in the Milky way. This shift is called Ayanamsa or Precession as in Sidereal (Vedic) system.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This Ayanamsa is used to put back the disk to the original position, which gets its &#8220;Start of Aries&#8221; point right.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Why this was done in Vedic is, the basics are in the Karmic theory of Rebirth and Death. So unless the disc or the horoscope is set back to its original zero-ith point, one cannot read the carry-over of Karma from previous births.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">With Start of Aries, calculated and made fixed for a year, the measurement of signs and stars, with constellations (STARs) AND Signs (Rashi), which are more or less stationery, from a geo-centric observations, is INDEPENDENT of seasons on Earth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So to summarize geometrically, Vedic Horoscope considers the movement of planets from a Karmic Point called Start of Aries, with constellations and Signs as the background for calculations.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Coming to Analysis, the different theories within Vedic Astrology is vast to predict, the actual karmic effects of a person, from his/her horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Western Astrology will stay in Earth only, as it depends only on seasons on Earth, so only psychological effects is possible, with it.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Albeit seasons changes on Earth at different places, esp, near South, North and Equator areas. So it cannot be Universal (on Earth). With seasons reference, measuring and something in sky, namely planets, is not scientific.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Vedic is ALWAYS superior than Western.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">BTW, Time delineation using Dasha can be found only in Sidereal Vedic.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So be it, Tathaastu.</p><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Image : Courtesy Google Images</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-9d560516ab993ae3bc6a17e562082ba4" master_src="/img/qimg-9d560516ab993ae3bc6a17e562082ba4" master_w="259" master_h="194" /></div></div></blockquote></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Nov 02, 2019 11:37 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Why is the law of karma inexorable?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Newton's third law is:</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>For every action, there is an equal and opposite reaction.</b></p></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=33a8d1&amp;url=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Newton%2527s_laws_of_motion" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="wikipedia.org">Newton's laws of motion - Bhukthi is the sub part of each Dasha. The division is based on sub-parts of 120 years of a graha. This is math.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Dasha is calculated on Chandra position. But Chandra itself is a Graha. Old text prescribe based on Chandra only. This is an approximation.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The fallacy of Vimshottari system is the above.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I differ. Timing an event should be purely be on math not on logic.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">One can see, logic is used to time an event, which is reverse-proof reading. Recently I read one. It goes as below</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Prathyantra lord is Budha who is third lord, so I write this now. Absurd.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Timing of Event DO NOT obey geometrical patterns of planets. But it is calculated based on position.</b></p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Nov 08, 2019 06:02 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the Sri Chakra mystery of Oregon, USA?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-9c1c3cec88ba5e0fc478789675af85ee" master_src="/img/qimg-9c1c3cec88ba5e0fc478789675af85ee" master_w="263" master_h="192" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Courtesy : Google images</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">One can know more about it in <span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=46728d&amp;url=https://www.google.com/search?q%3Dsri%2Bchakra%2Boregon" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="google.com">google search for Sri Chakra Oregon</a></span>.</p></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There had been counterclaims by some group, that they did it, but proved wrong by another.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As such Shri Chakra or Yantra is itself a Mystery. This can NOT be done on our Earth, as we are on Earth and when using geo-centric observation data for a horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So the nearest Graha is used in Vimshottari Dasha. And that Graha is Chandra.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/profile/Steve-Hora"><b><i>Read my Profile</i></b></a></span></p><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I challenge the status quo and ad-literam of vedic and western astrology, navigate uncharted waters, to find newer vistas from the astrology lore and find the truth. Period.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For example, Navamsa or D9 is a division of each house of D1 into 9 parts.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The parts are DISTRIBUTED to different &#8220;Houses&#8221;. That is it. Period.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Proof: As such the PARTS DO NOT become the WHOLE. So it stays as a part or Amsa.</p><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-ba63651044a740c5665bc7995b099428" master_src="/img/qimg-ba63651044a740c5665bc7995b099428" master_w="277" master_h="182" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Courtesy : Google Images</p></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But how to read the Amsa chart, and that, can be done, only by, erudite Astrologers, like me, not just referring back to old books to claim or deny otherwise.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It takes math and intuition to read Amsa charts, to know the meaning with respect to D1 chart.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Nov 12, 2019 08:26 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the 1 to 249 concept in KP astrology?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">249 number was arrived by KP, by dividing Placidus or Non-Equal house into parts using Vimshottari Dasha periods for each Graha.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>It is a flawed number. How?</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Vimshottari Dasha consists nine sub graha dashas, and further divided at antara level into 9. So totally it is 9 * 9 = 81.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are 3 sets of nakshatras for each graha in the zodiac.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So 81 * 3 = 243.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So the KP number SHOULD be 243 only.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But KP in his time was swayed by Western thought, deviated from Indian books, found his own ayanamsa, changed from Equal houses to Placidus and got a mixed thought as KP astrology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In KP, Un-Equal houses cannot have equal nakshatra degrees. But the Vimshottari Dasha is equal nakshatra system.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>There goes down the fallacy of KP Astrology.</b></p><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-2b2f148e3a1e57915cdaecd3c305be37" master_src="/img/qimg-2b2f148e3a1e57915cdaecd3c305be37" master_w="225" master_h="225" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Courtesy : Google Images.</p></blockquote></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Nov 13, 2019 05:27 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the Bhava Chalit chart?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Rashi or Lagna chart is based on &#8220;Start of Aries&#8221; and Equal Houses of Parasara system.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Bhava Chalit chart is based on Inter-Cuspal, In-equal Houses of SriPati of recent origin.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Sripati or Bhava or Chalit or KP or Placidus are just masturbation of a free mind. Some use Sripati to reverse-proof or fit their dasha or yoga prediction. Absurd and Quixotically.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Sripati or Bhava or Chalit or KP or Placidus cannot be used to derive Divisional charts.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I am reproducing the text from a web page for reference.</p><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Courtesy : ShreeAmbika</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>BHAVA SRIPATI CHART</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>How is a Bhava Chart Calculated?</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">To calculate bhava chart, we need two values &#8211; Ascendant and Mid heaven. Ascendant is the sign rising in the eastern direction at the time of casting of chart. The longitudinal position of Ascendant is the mid point of the first house. Mid heaven is the sign directly above the head. It is the midpoint of tenth house. The steps to calculate mid points of other houses are:</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">total difference = Ascendant &#8211; Midheaven</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">difference for one house = total difference divided by three</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">mid point of 11th house = midheaven + difference for one house</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">mid point of 12th house = mid point of 11th house + difference for one house.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Similarly, calculate the mid points of all the other houses to get the bhava chart. The starting point of a bhava is the mean of its and the previous house&#8217;s midpoint. Naturally, the end point of a house is the beginning of the next one.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>How is Rashi Chart different from Chalit Chart?</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>1. Mathematically:</b> Rashi chart assumes that all the houses are equal &#8211; 30 degrees in length. While calculating the positions of ascendant and other planets, we just take the modulo of the degree by 30 and assign the houses. In bhava chart, the mid point of a house, i.e. the bhava madhya, is given a lot of importance. The influence of a house is calculated based on this bhava madhya. e.g. if Ascendant value is 2 degrees, then the influence of the first house extends from approximately 350 degrees to about 17 degrees and not Zero to 30 degrees as would be the case with a rashi chart. The upper and the lower limits of influence of a house are called Bhava Sandhis. Planets are placed in this newly computed Bhava chart &#8211; and we get something called Chalit chart. The rule is simple, if a planet&#8217;s longitude is more than the starting sandhi and less than the end sandhi, it is said to fall in that bhava.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>2. For interpretations:</b> The combinations that are used for interpretations are &#8211; rashi chart along with divisional charts on one hand and bhava charts on other hand. We never mix divisional charts with bhava chart. Planets influence a chart based on the bhava they are situated in. Rule of thumb &#8211; if an interpretation system works only with planets and houses and not signs, you can safely assume that it is working with the chalit chart and not the rashi chart. However, the aspects of planets on other planets are always studied from rashi chart. Similarly exaltation/debilitation of planets is again studied only from the rashi chart. Manglik Dosha is studied partly from bhava chart (e.g. statements like Mars causes dosha if situated in 7th house) and partly from rashi chart. When looking for exceptions (e.g. Mars in Simha, i.e. in the sign of a friend does not cause dosha), we should see the rashi chart. Normally, bhava chart and rashi chart would agree with each other. However, if the Ascendant or planets&#8217; degree is closer to multiple of 30, there may be differences between the charts. It is always interesting to see if a planet has moved from one house to another from rashi chart to chalit chart. This explains a lot of times why a yoga that is so obvious in rashi chart does not fructify in real life.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="portrait qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-efa6a2b1995a4dff7c5b5f81098e8c99" master_src="/img/qimg-efa6a2b1995a4dff7c5b5f81098e8c99" master_w="215" master_h="235" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Courtesy : Google Image.</p></blockquote></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Nov 13, 2019 09:43 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">How will the Guru Transit (November 2019) into Dhanur affect a Vrischika Rashi person?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The benevolent Guru, will move from Vrischika to Dhanur on Nov 5th 2019, as per panchang.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Dhanur Rashi</b> House contains the following nakshatra namely</p><ol><li>Moola - 1,2,3,4th pada - Ruled by Ketu</li><li>Purva Shada(Puram) - 1,2,3,4 pada Ruled by Shukra</li><li>Uttara Shada (Uttiradam) - 1 pada Ruled by Surya</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">and Guru will transit the above nakshatras.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Vrischika Rashi consists of the following nakshatras namely</b></p><ul><li>Visakha - 4th pada - Ruled by Guru</li><li>Anuradha (Anusham) - 1,2,3,4 pada Ruled by Shani</li><li>Jyeshta (Ketai) - 1,2,3,4 pada Ruled by Budha</li></ul><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ascertain your Rashi and then your nakshtra and then read your affectations.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Guru transiting the 2nd from Vrischika Rasi is good , overall. 100% accurate,</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Logic - Depends based on method and astrologer,</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Connecting the dots - Depends again based on method and astrologer.</p><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-82d090186cbc69b938ed65c37ee60339" master_src="/img/qimg-82d090186cbc69b938ed65c37ee60339" master_w="290" master_h="173" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Courtesy : Google Images</p></blockquote></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Nov 16, 2019 05:36 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Isn't the degree of a planet necessary for deciding debilitation or exaltation in a particular sign?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-1a702a577df6623587e7e4f9a0cc46f4" master_src="/img/qimg-1a702a577df6623587e7e4f9a0cc46f4" master_w="632" master_h="246" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><i>Image Source:</i> Goravani Jyotish</p></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The degree of a planet is necessary for deciding debilitation or exaltation in a particular sign or house.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">That said, the horoscope is a snapshot of Graha-movement at the time of birth of a person or event. Kind of still photograph.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The grahas continue to move, even after the said birth or event. This brings the transit effects on the said still photo or horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The power of the each graha as in above table, shows 100% at deep exalted or debilitated degrees.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It decreases on both sides of exalted degrees, like a mount, according to sthana bala of that graha.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It increases on both sides of debilitated degrees, like a trough, according to sthana bala of that graha.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In this scenario, the power can increase or decrease and cross over to adjacent signs or houses.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This is where most astrologers get confused.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>There goes down another fallacy of Vedic Astrology.</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">To read with graha exaltation or debilitation inside a house, as well its influence on other adjacent houses, using sthana bala, can be done only using math, by erudite astrologer and reseacher like me.</p><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-f0ff5395ca8b22185ebaacdea4daa813" master_src="/img/qimg-f0ff5395ca8b22185ebaacdea4daa813" master_w="287" master_h="176" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><i>Image Source:</i> Google Images</p></blockquote></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Nov 26, 2019 05:59 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is biorythm in astrology? sign?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In Tamil or Vedic Astrology and in Tamil Calendar, every month, full Moon is celebrated.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The tamil calendar is based on Sidereal Sun months.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The phases of moon for each day is called Tithi in Tamil.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Full Moon is called Pournami.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><i>Panguni Uthiram</i> means Sun-month (Panguni) from 15th March to 15th April, a full moon transits through the star or asterism or nakshatra called Uthiram. Uthiram star belongs to Leo partly and Virgo Moon sign.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So a Full Moon (Pournami) tithi occurs in the above month and said Moon sign.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As per Tamil Hindu calendar, this tithi-month combination is auspicious.</p><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="portrait qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-640eca6e48ede4c5ae4eec3db6940393" master_src="/img/qimg-640eca6e48ede4c5ae4eec3db6940393" master_w="197" master_h="256" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Courtesy : Google Image.</p></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The significance is great.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For e.g.: Lord Buddha born as Siddarth, was born on a Poornima, got Enlightened on a Poornima and attained the end (Samadhi) on a Poornima.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So be it. Tathaastu.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Dec 14, 2019 05:46 AM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the Tithi Pravesha Chakra for the monthly and yearly return of the Moon?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Sun (Soul) is considered as Father in Vedic Astrology and Moon (Mind) as Mother for this Earth and its Earthlings, born in an ascendant (Body).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So it is imperative to consider the difference of degrees between Sun and Moon, which is nothing but Tithi, an observed astronomical phenomenon, happening daily in the sky, as the basis of any Return of the Monthly or Yearly.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">VarshaPhal of any Solar Calendar in India, is based on Sun&#8217;s return, likewise a Yearly or Monthly return of Chandra or Moon, based on Tithi is called Tithi Pravesha Chakra.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Why Tithi is so important?.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Adhi-Shakthi&#8217;s Maha Vidya of Shri Chakra is based on Tithi. When such is the prowess of the creator of Universe, Tithi becomes the de-facto of any birth or event on Earth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So be it. Tathaastu.</p><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-c8cc3fac47cf5f4b78263207787f7c0b" master_src="/img/qimg-c8cc3fac47cf5f4b78263207787f7c0b" master_w="226" master_h="223" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Courtesy : Google Images - Fifteen Nityas</p></blockquote></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Dec 14, 2019 08:14 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is it like to be a professional astrologer?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I take inspiration from Karen Marie Shelton, another answerer to this question. Thanks Karen.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>**My First Shingle**</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I started learning Vedic Astrology from my Father&#8217;s brother. He taught me how to read Panchang and introduced to books and taught the basics. My age was at that time 17 years. I am now more than 3 times this number.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>**Private discussions**</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There was private predictions with Kith, Kin and Friends about astrology, to understand Nadi leaf readings, its secrets and its methodology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>**Astrological Research and Consultations**</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I was into research of vedic astrology, as I started as a non-believer of fate and destiny. (Ketu in my lagna).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Books helped to understand different prediction techniques. Condensing them, understanding the noun, verb, adjective of a prediction was my first challenge. Then came the very timing.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I was not satisfied with Vimshottari dasha for timing, based on Moon. So more research was done by me, to come up with a unique system.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Remedies was again a challenge that has to given, from a psychological and spiritual level.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">All these were done, as a part-time work with my engineering day job.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Being an engineer by profession, mathematical proof of any astrological axiom or its meta-physical meaning of the Sanskrit sutras, was my primary concern.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>**Doing Astrological Consultations Can Be Exhausting**</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It is challenging and exhausting, but the feedback from my followers made me changes, in my pattern of prediction, and was more or less standardized.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>**Long Term Clients**</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Clients return back now and then for newer problems, know their fate and find a solution to their life events.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">**Hard Work And Potentially Frustrating**</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It was a lot of long years of lonely path of learning, hard work and thinking, which frustrates.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>**Electional Astrology**</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As this is a easy one in Vedic astrology with the help of Panchang. Vara and weekday, I ignore, as it does not contain any mathematical proof. Nor Hora dependent on Vara is used by me.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>**Mundane Astrology**</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This was exiting for me, to understand, how each graha shows its true character, in a worldly way, than imparting only color for human horoscopes.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>**Trying To Warn Clients May Be Futile**</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Well, the self-confidence of each client, makes them think that they can overcome, any bad or negative prediction. This is a shortcoming of most.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>**Destiny And Free Will Are Important**</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As I had my dive into Western astrology, it was easy for me to understand and explain, to clients, what is free will and what one is destined to be.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>**Preparation Is Critical For Some Professional Astrologers**</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It is true that preparation, be good at basics, apply the same axioms for all horoscopes for prediction, use the same mathematical timing for different houses for different events, is needed. This took my time.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>**Drawbacks And Rewards**</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There is NO great income in this thankless job. Very few understands that.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Only one lady (client) understood that, and she sends Guru dakshina every year, without me asking for it. I bless her, with the divine in me.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The reward to throw light (Jyoti) on one&#8217;s karma, by predicting, is the highlight of this thankless divine science.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So be it, Tathaastu.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Pranam to all the Gurus of Jyotish. _/\_</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Dec 17, 2019 07:38 AM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">How do I calculate the daily thithis based on the location one is residing? </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">How do you time events in Dasha?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Dasha systems are many in Vedic Astrology for timing events in one&#8217;s life from the horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Each Dasha system has a purpose as enumerated in the samhitas.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-057f1020965fd836acb88b4895326441" master_src="/img/qimg-057f1020965fd836acb88b4895326441" master_w="310" master_h="163" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are general purpose dasha sytems namely Vimshottari and Ashtottari Dasha systems.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Both are nakshatra based, meaning the position of Chandra is taken for initial reminder dasha calculation.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Vimshottari is 120 years and Asshtottari is 108 years based.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I will dwell upon Vimshottari as it uses 120 years which is normally accepted as the maximum age that a human can live. Also the zodiac is 360 degree, which is a multiple of 120.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Again the 120 is divided into equal number of nakshatras namely 9.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are variations of Vimshottari with their own bylaws, which I will NOT consider for now.</p><ul><li>The lord of the nakshatra is NOT the lord of a House.</li><li>The dasha lord is NOT the same as the lord of a house.</li><li>Same goes for Antara or sub-antara periods.</li><li>The graha(s) in a nakshatra is NOT connected to Dasha lords.</li><li>Timing is pure maths and NOT logic of yoga or any graha placed in some nakshatra.</li></ul><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For example : Some would say -&gt; Guru is in Shani nakshatra, Guru dasha is running, Shani antara, Shani is 7th lord, so marriage will happen. This kind of analysis or synthesis is ABSURD.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When Space (Graha degree in zodiac) meets the Time or Samaya (Dasha) for a particular Event lord, then the timing calculated, will make that event happen.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Feb 05, 2020 07:54 AM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What happens if both the bride and the groom have the same Upapada Lagna?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Upapada lagna clearly denotes 12th lord significance of a chart.</p><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">What you get out of your spouse or you giving her/him. How I do?.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When reading a horoscope, a vedic one, there are two parts.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>First Part is Prediction</b>: One is the reading based on the position of Grahas, and its significance with respect to houses, signs, nakshatras and most importantly Amsa (Divisional charts).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The above para is about the metaphysical meaning of the horoscope to the life events. This can vary depending on the methodology followed by the Astrologer and his/her experience and adeptness.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>My method</b>: I use Vedic (Sidereal) horoscope for Accurate timing and analysis, according to Lahiri Ayanamsa (Chitra paksha), using sidereal solar years of 360, Analysis is as per Parasara system.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Second Part is the timing of events</b>:</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This is the crux part and math is involved, which should be scientific.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I use the same timing algorithm for all events of each houses and for any horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Example : Timing for health is from 1st house and for Career it is 10th house. Both time period running parallel with different overlapping time periods.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Not one Mahadasa </b>or antara taking care of both 1st and 10th. <b>That is crappy.</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This way there will be 12 dasha-antara running parallel for all the 12 houses.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This explains some of the crude logic of life, namely, a person will be earning a lot, but simultaneously suffering from a disease. </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">How is the D60 chart analyzed by the KP method?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">D60 ShastiAmsa chart is a divisional or amsa or varga chart derived from D1 Lagna Chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">KP method is NOT connected to D60 chart at all, nor KP method can analyse D60.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">KP method is a technique for timing, and it is a callous one at that.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">How?</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">KP assumes that 120 years of VImshottari Dasha can be divided in 249 parts.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Funnily 249 is wrong.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">How?</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The 120 degree of the zodiac is divided into 9 nakshatras of 13 deg 20 min each. Each nakshatra is again divided into 9 parts.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So total is 9 * 9 = 81.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are 3 * 120&#8217;s in a zodiac.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So grand total is 81 * 3 = 243.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">249 is wrong and only 243 is mathematically correct.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So KP is callously wrong in timing, mathematically, at the basic level. And it uses non-equal Placidus house system borrowed from western, to suit at that time of popularity. Non-Equal houses CANNOT generate any Amsa chart, even a simple NavaAmsa chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Also it considers some cuspal theory and tropical calculations, to be more appropriate in his time towards western thinking.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" Fame: How does astrology predict that one will become wealthy and famous?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">2nd house is the indicator of all wealth in astrology chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">All connections to 2nd house particular to a chart denotes the way the wealth got.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Any 2nd house lord of any house indicates wealth got from that house.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">e.g. 11th is 2nd from 10th,so gains from career (10th) is denoted by 11th and its lord.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Where it is posited, in which nakshatra, in which amsa, in which kalaa and in which dasha, denotes the amount, way, acceptance, time and nature of manas, the wealth is got.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Famous is denoted by 5th house.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jul 02, 2020 07:35 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What are nakshatras? What is the scientific explanation for them?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As <span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/profile/Rami-Sivan">Rami Sivan</a></span> had explained in his answer, nakshatra is just a finer division of the zodiac.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Nakshatra in vedic astrology, can be a single or a group of stars (constellation).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The metaphysical meaning of Nakshatra is what makes the difference in prediction.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So when Chandra traverses a particular Nakshatra, a particular character was observed for a person born in that period of Chandra. So those attributes were assigned to that person as having it.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">A such a nakshatra does NOT by itself gives attributes to a person.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The nakshatra was given a Graha name for codification, and as such that Graha also is not for attributes of the person.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But at a house level, there are portfolios which house governs.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jul 02, 2020 07:53 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is your opinion of the astrologer PVR Narasimha Rao, his software Jagannatha Hora and his delineation of the Pushya-paksha Ayanamsa?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">PVR Narasimha Rao Garu had done a great exemplary service and Punya to Vedic Astrology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">He is the Seer of Modern Vedic Astrology after B.V.Raman. class="rendered_qtext">What are the Mantra, Yantra, and Tantra?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Mantra, Yantra and Tantra are esoteric things for Sadhana.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Mantra is the Sound Energy.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Yantra is the Space and Energy - namely body, its chakras and geometric shapes of 2D and 3D as idols or Chakras.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Tantra is the procedure - namely yoga, astrological things like nakshatra, tithi etc namely Time.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Each of these three has varied meaning in every context.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Astrological context is again mixed with many things.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For example : Graha Shanti Puja uses grains, nakshatra at tantra level. Idol of Graha at Yantra level and Graha mantra for the puja.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Space, Energy and Time are ones that has to be connected to Mantra, Yantra and Tantra, astrologically.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Space governs Eye and Ear and its properties namely Seeing and Hearing.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Energy is the body which gives energy to the mantra uttered.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Time is calculated from the horoscope to customize the Tantra.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When these are synced, then the Karma of a person dissolves, good or bad.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shri Chakra is the one, when customized to a person&#8217;s horoscope, brings about this.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="portrait qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-ec9254153c3c74cef5dab45ad6e7f005" master_src="/img/qimg-ec9254153c3c74cef5dab45ad6e7f005" master_w="898" master_h="908" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So be it. Is this true?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It is true that Rahu and Ketu does go anti-clockwise in a horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Normally, the parikrama that is done in a Nava Griha is 9 times clockwise.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Your question is valid. But one has to go into details of the placements of graha idols in a Hindu temple for Parikrama purposes.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are two school of thoughts about the placements.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The one followed in Tamil Nadu is the correct one. Is DigBala applicable to Navamsa as well?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Digbala means directional strength acquired by a said planet or graha. The different houses represents different directions.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Lagna is East, as the Ascendant or Rising point is measured using Sun, so East. The measured value will be different., based on a lagna lord planet&#8217;s placement in that directional house.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Digbala is measured for Lagna or Rashi chart only.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But the ascendant gets a particular significance or Amsa as per the divisional chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In Nava-Amsa chart DigBala of the ascendant gets a significance, but the basic strength is still from D1 or lagna chart only.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">e.g.: If say Simha as lagna. Look for Surya and where in which house placed. Based on that, the DigBala of Surya is calculated. If Surya is placed in Simha, both in Rashi and Navamsa, then Surya gets highest DigBala and a significance of Vargottama in Navamsa.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Aug 28, 2020 03:35 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Can a Western astrologer use the sidereal system?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">A Western Astrologer need NOT use the sidereal system and there is NO necessity for that.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As western astrology do NOT take into account the precession of equinox into consideration.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Once upon a time the tropical (western) and sidereal (Vedic) coincided and was the same. The drift started happening due to astronomical reasons, which Vedic takes into account, using a reference point, namely a fixed star (e.g. Spica).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are different values due to different reference point and in the calculation of <b>Ayanamsa or Precession of Equinox</b>.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Western Astrology is grounded to Earth with its reference to Solstice, which makes it very effective in analyzing the natural tendencies and psychology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Vedic syncs back to the old reference point, by minus the Ayanamsa, which makes it good for analyzing the Karmic deeds of a person and its ensuing yoga in this birth.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Aug 30, 2020 06:18 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What will be the impact from tomorrow's rarest of the planetary combination starting at 10:30 AM Sep 13th, 2020 on different lagnas?  8 planets out of 9 will be sitting in their own sign for next 60 hours.</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Excellent observation. class="rendered_qtext">Is Navamsa used to determine the strength of the planet in rasi chart or used to tell life after 36 of native?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Many many fine Astrologers had written about this new research, both on Quora and on Internet.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There is no proof or Sanskrit verse, which substantiates this &#8220;After 36&#8221; assumption.</p><ol><li>All divisional charts are DERIVED from Lagna chart, so everything and anything STARTS with Lagna chart.</li><li>BUT for a particular significance (e.g: Marriage, Karma - Navamsa - D9), the karmic destiny becomes more activated. Again this significance is read in reference with D1 or Lagna chart.</li><li>In South India, Rashi (Lagna) and Navamsa are the only charts used for a quick Naadi reading for General Kandam of Palm Leaf, which gives a glimpse of the whole life.</li><li>Other divisional charts like D10 Dasamsa is read with D1 chart for Career.</li><li>With D1 and all divisional charts, life opens like a flower with all its petals.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Now how to clear this myth of &#8220;After 36&#8221;. Simple.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Number 9 is very significant in Hinduism and Vedic Astrology, as in Nava(9)Amsa.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Each house has 9 navamsa pada. By distributing them to each Graha, a full cycle gets completed within a house. This cycle repeats in the next and next houses.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As per Navamsa Dasha system, each Amsa is given a year, totaling to 108 years of Life or Ayush.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For one full house cycle, it will be 9 years. For one quadrant for example : from Mesha till Karkataka it will be 36 years. Why one quadrant, one may ask, it is 120 years of Vimshottari Dasha is used for 9 set of planets.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So the first 36 years, the Navamsa significance is NOT visible or Tangible, due to the fact, that All Grahas had not fully karmic matured for Space (Houses), Energy (Planets) and Time (Dasha).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The next 36 year cycle shows tangible karmic influences. The analogy being the flower opens with the next set of petals, as it unfolds.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So NAVAMSA has to be read with Lagna chart from birth till death, with intuition for different cycles of it.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-018e4b7014c5e5c34e0fcc6b91293f80" master_src="/img/qimg-018e4b7014c5e5c34e0fcc6b91293f80" master_w="274" master_h="137" /></div></div></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Sep 24, 2020 08:47 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Do Neechabhanga rules apply to debilitated planets in Navamsa? How can one interpret the results from Neecha Bhanga happening in Navasam?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Neechabhanga or Debilitation or Exaltation rules DOES NOT apply for Navamsa or ANY divisional chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Debilitation or Exaltation is with respect to degrees in Lagna chart. When a derived chart like Navamsa is made out of Lagna chart, the degree meaning loses all its value as such in divisional chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The said debilitated gets a newer significance in the Navamsa chart as placed in that Navamsa. For eg: Vargottama.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Yes, Vargottama has the power to cancel debilitation in a way equivalent to Neechabhanga in Lagna chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But transposing Neecha or its bhanga to Navamsa is against Math and meta-physics of Astrology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The myth of this assumption would have come about as follows</p><ol><li>All divisional charts look like Lagna chart, which is NOT technically or mathematically correct.</li><li>In a cyclic way the divisions of a divisional chart (Navamsa) are distributed in a 12 house fashion.</li><li>The 12 houses of a Lagna DOES NOT correspond to the 12 houses of any divisional chart.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Rather the division of an Amsa has more significance than the house concerned. Like in case of Vargottama.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Sep 25, 2020 07:21 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Is there any way to know your past karma through astrology?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Karma is Action. Its fruits are Punya and Papa, depending on the nature of it.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">A Personal Astrological Birth Chart is a map of the Past Karma's of a Person. The chart is made with Planetary Positions at the Time of Birth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Karma creates Papa (Bad debt) and Punya (Good vibes).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">One is born to enjoy Punya and suffer Papa.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">One of the divisional chart namely D60 - ShastiAmsa delineates the Past Karma of the Past birth(s).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Another one D150 - NadiAmsa captures the whole present life with its Karma and its output namely Papa and Puya.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-c8e73bba6f96ba4da2f549c936f3d336" master_src="/img/qimg-c8e73bba6f96ba4da2f549c936f3d336" master_w="240" master_h="72" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But making these charts need accurate Time of Birth, Best Ayanamsa, Scientific Ephemeris and a good analytical mind to analyse, interpret, synthesis and predict.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Astrology with Houses (Space), Planets (Energy), Time (Dasha) and Karma can predict Past, Present and Future.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Sep 29, 2020 05:27 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What are the astrological results for an exalted Mercury?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The question is about Astrological results about exalted Budha or Mercury.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Not to a particular birth chart. Period.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Budha is exalted in its own house, which is Kanya and owns it also. This is a very salient feature of this Graha and stands out from other grahas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Even the most powerful Grahas like Surya, Guru and Shani do not have this bala.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Within Kanya Rashi, there are three nakshatras namely Uttara, Hasta and Chitra.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The deep exaltation of Budha is at 15 degrees, right in the middle of the Rashi and in Hasta nakshatra 2nd pada.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Chandra owns the 11th house from Kanya. So Budha gets maximum benefit from Chandra, even if it is a temporal enemy of Chandra.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So Budha gives maximum benefit in Virgo or Kanya, with its exaltation and house ownership power.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Even if Budha is neecha and sitting in Meena, and looking at its own house, it gives best benefits.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">From the above statement one can know what Neecha Grahas can also give benefits.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Budha exalted in a horoscope, has altogether a different meaning, and depends on other factors of Budha.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-95fd8c9c7b6e18f48bc85649feb8c361" master_src="/img/qimg-95fd8c9c7b6e18f48bc85649feb8c361" master_w="239" master_h="90" /></div></div></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Oct 02, 2020 01:54 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What are the rules of analysing a native's annual Tithi Pravesha chakra?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Tithi </b>is the angular distance between Surya (Sun) and Chandra (Moon), which is nothing but the phases of Chandra as waxing and waning.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Poornima </b>(Full Moon) is when Chandra is 180 degrees opposite to Surya. And <b>Amavasya </b>(New Moon) is when Chandra hides behind Earth from Surya, in its rotation.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are 15 phases or tithis. From Amavasya till Poornima it is called <b>Shukla Paksha </b>(waxing) (Brighter Phase) and from Poornima till Amavasya is called <b>Krishna Paksha </b>(Dark Phase).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">A person is born in a particular Tithi, which is called Janma Tithi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As life progresses year to year, the same tithi in that same lunisolar month happens. That return of the same tithi is called Tithi Pravesha and its associated chakra or chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The significance is as below</p><ol><li>Surya and Chandra plays an important role on Earth</li><li>The angular distance or tithi influences the body and mind.</li><li>The return of the same tithi signifies the same composition as at janma or birth.</li><li>The lagna and other grahas would have changed places, but given the importance of Surya and Chandra, the effects on this tithi-born person can be predicted for that year.</li><li>The Tithi Pravesha is extended to each month of the Year also, and a monthly prediction on tithi can be done.</li><li>The tithi has connection to Space (Houses), Energy (Grahas), Time (Tithi) and Karma and it is a secret, which cannot be divulged.</li><li>With Tithi one can change life course of the Karma-based lagna chart with its Papa/Punya outputs.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>The rules of analysis</b></p><ul><li>Janma Tithi and present Tithi Pravesha for year or month should be same with remaining tithi percentage.</li><li>The position of Lagna, Surya and Chandra should be noted in Lagna and Tithi Pravesha chart.</li><li>The disposition of these with each, of its own, will tell whether it is a good or bad year or month.</li><li>Using Ashtottari Tithi Dasha system for that year, one can predict for that year.</li></ul><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-8ea2ec533b53f1a0cf3a319f907ea25c" master_src="/img/qimg-8ea2ec533b53f1a0cf3a319f907ea25c" master_w="245" master_h="147" /></div></div></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Oct 04, 2020 05:08 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span And how to interpret my ascendent, do Vedic and Western interpret Gemini ascendent similarly?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Birth chart in Vedic Astrology (Sidereal) Planetary &amp; Ascendant position = Western Tropical position - Ayanamsa (Precession of Equinox).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Due to above formula, ascendant can be in Gemini in Vedic and Cancer in Western.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Vedic chart is predisposed to predict the actual karma from birth to birth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The western is about the free will with which to act upon in this life.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The effort put to overcome the inertia of karma is what makes one strive with free will.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">With Western one can understand, what is the possibility for free will and with Vedic, what are the available karmic possibilities in life.</p><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-5763ef4697cb988a81395276adde206b" master_src="/img/qimg-5763ef4697cb988a81395276adde206b" master_w="275" master_h="183" /></div></div></blockquote></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Oct 07, 2020 01:25 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What's the easiest way to predict events using vedic astrology?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The easiest way of predicting is using Sudarshana Chakra Dasha in Vedic Astrology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Definition</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Sudarshana Chakra used by Lord Vishnu has 108 spokes and the emblem of Lord Jaganath of Puri temple.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">108 signifies Navamsa padas. In another Q2A, a brief about Navamsa as below</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/Is-Navamsa-used-to-determine-the-strength-of-the-planet-in-rasi-chart-or-used-to-tell-life-after-36-of-native/answer/Steve-Hora">Steve Hora's answer to Is Navamsa used to determine the strength of the planet in rasi chart or used to tell life after 36 of native?</a></span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Procedure</b></p><ol><li>Take the Navamsa D9 chart.</li><li>Check for the position of Grahas in Lagna chart, whether it is in Moveable, Dual or Fixed sign.</li><li>Check the same in Navamsa.</li><li>Take one luni-solar year for each Navamsa.</li><li>A luni-solar day is tithi not a solar day as observed every day now.</li><li>Make the Sudarshan Chakra Dasha Timing based on Lagna, Surya or Chandra using good software.</li><li>The initial left over years at birth for Surya, Lagna and Chandra will tell position in Navamsa.</li><li>From that position count number of years for each house or sign.</li><li>Based on the Dasha and the number of Navamsa count, one can predict the event of life.</li></ol><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-1d0ba4ec96466ed9d2b7d1a84cd83dc0" master_src="/img/qimg-1d0ba4ec96466ed9d2b7d1a84cd83dc0" master_w="237" master_h="236" /></div></div></blockquote></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Oct 09, 2020 04:49 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Which Sidereal Ayanamsa is most accurate?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><a id="cite-JiFDJ" href="#JiFDJ" class="citation_link">[1]</a> Sideral Ayanamsa or Precession of Equinox can be a frustrating one to determine given the below astronomical reasons.</p><ol><li>The Earth wobbles</li><li>The Moon&#8217;s perturbation on Earth&#8217;s movement</li><li>The Sun&#8217;s pull on both Earth and Moon</li><li>Sun&#8217;s own movement around the center of the milkyway galaxy.</li><li>Measuring these NOT from Earth, instead using a reference in space.</li><li>Then when the two zodiacs namely Sidereal and Tropical coincided</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>A scientific approach</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Ayanamsa - A Scientific Calculation as the most accurate one.</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Scientific data : </b>Data used is from scientific community and not from Vedic text books.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But Vedic Seers have to be credited for noting this great scientific data namely Ayanamsa or Precession of Equinox, astronomically long back. This is the greatest Achievement of Vedic Sidereal Astrology and Astronomical observations in India from time immemorial.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=925fa6&amp;url=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Axial_precession" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="wikipedia.org">Axial precession - Wikipedia</a></span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Calculation of Ayanamsa using Modern Astronomical Data</b></p><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Polaris (Alpha UMi) or Urs Major or Dhrurva nakshatra or the Pole star is the present reference star for measuring the precession of Earth or Ayanamsa.</p></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">North Ecliptic Pole (NEP) is 90 degree of center of Equator of Earth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Earth tilt is about 23 degrees 26 min 11.8 seconds (23.43661 degrees). Again this changes slightly due to Earth nutations, but more or less constant. So, North Celestial Pole (NCP) of Earth is in a tilt of 23.43661 degree with NEP of Earth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Also the Polaris star is tilted from NCP (NCP-Polaris tilt) by 0.736 degrees away. This value will change according to Earths nutation and Polaris own motion.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Scientifically according to mathematical calculation, NCP will point and will be closet to Polaris in 2140 AD.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The full precession circle of Dhurva or Polaris nakshatra, scientifically is 25,771.58 Julian years. In Hindu terminology it is 25,770 years.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The scientific accumulated precession formula for 2000 as the epoch Julian year is</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>AP = 5,028.796195 + 2.2108696 &#215; T in ArcSeconds, T being the Julian centuries.</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So to use this above formula, we need to know when the tropical and sidereal zodiac coincided.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">25771.58 minus 2140 years will take us back in time, when Polaris was in same position as it will be in 2140, meaning NCP will be exactly pointing to Polaris with zero tilt with NCP, that is (25771.58 - 2140) = 23631.58 julian years back.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So the total Julian years expended from that NCP-Polaris-Zero year, is used to calculate the total accumulated precession.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">23631.58 plus 2000 = 25631.58, will enable us to use above formula for Epoch 2000 which is the scientific formula for <b>Accumulated precession</b>.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Accumulated Precession (AP) in ArcSeconds AP = 5,028.796195 + 2.2108696 * ( 23631.58 minus 2000) / 365.25) dividing with 365.25 is done to convert normal number of years to Julian years.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The values got from above has to be added to the actual tilt of Earth w.r.t to Dhurva nakshatra on that day, i.e. Epoch 2000.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Why add, one may ask, it is because the Earth arrives later (Or Sun arrives earlier) to same point on celestial plane around Sun, due to this precession.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Adding 23.43661 tilt degree (between NCP and NEP) will give Ayanamsa for Epoch 2000.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So, Ayanamsa = 23.43661 + (AP / 3600). AP is divided by 3600 to convert Arcseconds to degrees for Epoch 2000.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So the perfect scientific Ayanamsa formula for 2000 AD year is</p><ul><li>For birth year before 2000 Epoch</li></ul><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Ay = 23.43661 + (5,028.796195 + 2.2108696 * ( 23631.58 + (2000 - Birth Year) / 365.25)) / 3600</b></p><ul><li>For birth year after 2000 Epoch</li></ul><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Ay = 23.43661 + (5,028.796195 + 2.2108696 * ( 23631.58 + ((2000 - Birth Year) + (Birth Year - 2000)) / 365.25)) / 3600</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The slight changes in Earth tilt (Axial Tilt) changes between 22.1 and 24.5 degrees on a scale of 41000 years.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">and Polaris actual degree away from NCP now (40 arcminute or 0.736 degree away), again changes in few arcseconds, needs to be taken into consideration, which would be another calculation for another day.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=b5247a&amp;url=https://owd.tcnj.edu/~pfeiffer/AST261/AST261Chap4,Preces.pdf" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="tcnj.edu">More on Axial Precession</a></span></p><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If these two (Axial Tilt and NCP-Polaris Tilt) changes are taken into account, according to that Birth Year, it will make the aynamasa accurate in seconds. For that need more astronomical data, energy and time.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="portrait qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-065cf0a7257f69b10ec35754a29b6dbd" master_src="/img/qimg-065cf0a7257f69b10ec35754a29b6dbd" master_w="208" master_h="243" /></div></div></blockquote><p class="qtext_citation_lead">Footnotes</p><p class="citation" id="JiFDJ"><a href="#cite-JiFDJ" class="citation_index">[1] </a><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=9ffd54&amp;url=https://stevehora.com/blog/ayanamsa/" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="stevehora.com">Ayanamsa | Hora Vedic Astrology by Steve - Advice Predictions</a></span></p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Oct 10, 2020 10:20 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">How can I know my correct birth time for preparing a correct horoscope?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Using PranaPada Lagna</b> which is 20 times faster than the movement of Lagna point in a horoscope. Both the lagnas are based on Surya&#8217;s position on that day and the rotation of Earth upon itself in a day.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Basic Vedic Astrological math is needed to calculate the above lagna as below</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="render_latex">[math]1 solar day = 24 hours.[/math]</span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="render_latex">[math]1 solar day = 60 ghati.[/math]</span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="render_latex">[math]1 hora = 2.5 ghati.[/math]</span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="render_latex">[math]1 ghati = 60 vighati.[/math]</span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="render_latex">[math]1 minute   = 2.5 vighati.[/math]</span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Input for calculation</b></p><ol><li>Surya&#8217;s longitude at sunrise for that day of birth, in deg-min-sec.</li><li>Surya&#8217;s rising or sun rise-time for that day.</li><li>Note Surya&#8217;s position in chart, whether in Moveable, Fixed or Dual.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Procedure</b></p><ol><li>Find the difference between birth time and sun rise time in minutes, Diff-Min = BT<span class="render_latex">[math]~SRT[/math]</span>.</li><li>Convert that value to vighati, Diff-Min in vg.</li><li>Divide the above vighati value by 15.</li><li>The resultant value should be converted to degree-minutes-seconds.</li><li>Add this degree-min-sec to Surya&#8217;s sunrise longitude. Multiples of 12 at degree should be minus or expunged.</li><li>The above added figure need correction for different types of signs in which Surya is.</li><li>If Surya is in Moveable, add zero. If in Fixed, add 240 deg. If in Dual, add 120 degree.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Correction of TOB</b></p><ol><li>The above got Prana Pada has predictions based on its position from Surya&#8217;s Lagna, for Prana&#8217;s energy, attitude of person and type of vasana (smell) for wealth.</li><li>The Prana Pada should be in Trine or Trikona with Chandra, which indicates a Human birth. It is zodiac&#8217;s 360 * 2 is the speed of Hora.</li><li>Add above value to sunrise&#8217;s longitude.</li><li>The arrived value is Hora Lagna in that house of the zodiac.</li><li>Expunge 30&#8217;s from above value, to get the exact position in that house.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are predictions available for the Hora lagna to be in different houses from Rashi lagna.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-60ad1a3ba578a2edd0c17a9f44cb6f03"
