That does NOT mean that the Pada becomes a house.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Rather the Pada gets the Amsa / Influence / Significance of that house.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This very definition makes one read Navamsa chart reading, the proper way.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For Example : For Aswini nakshatra is as below</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-678ca68f38ec96a52ea52d80711acc42" master_src="/img/qimg-678ca68f38ec96a52ea52d80711acc42" master_w="257" master_h="115" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For other Nakshatra the above pattern extends till Revati.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Dec 23, 2020 05:36 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Why is astrology considered a pseudo-science?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Astrology is an Art not a Science.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Art cannot be replicated, analysed in a straight jacket rules and laws, with the likes of Science.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Astrology is a search for evidence and proof, not to get proved by some other set of rules of science. Period.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Reading just with lagna these classifications is generic to lagna not to other houses.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Lagna being Body and Mind, tends to get affected accordingly by these type of categorizations.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 03, 2021 09:19 AM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Can you analyse the horoscope of Queen Velu Nachiyar, Ramanathapuram, Tamil Nadu, the first freedom fighter against Britishers in India? Funny.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">To decide whether Saturn and other planets are good or bad, a horoscope has the following permutation and combinations</p><ol><li>12 houses, so 12 lagnas.</li><li>9 planets, so 9 * 12 combination of placement of planets in different lagnas.</li><li>9 planetary combinations, so 9 * 9 different combinations.</li><li>Special drishtis, can add more.</li><li>Other placement in nakshatra and varga charts, add more complexity.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">These above permutations may amount to more than a thousand, and its effect can be varying on an uneven time period called Dashas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So the effect of good or bad of any planets on a daily basis as manifestation is complex and uneven time based.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Planetary transits are equal in time period, but its effect on a horoscope is transitory or temporary.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Given the above scenario, a daily manifestation of these grahas and classifying it as its own good or bad, is complex, useless and not practical.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But there is way out.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 09, 2021 07:21 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the astrological significance of Tamil Pongal on January 14, 2021?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Tamil Pongal festival is celebrated by Tamils. Ojas is responsible for the body&#8217;s immunity and strength. It is destroyed by anger, over-exertion, malnutrition and lack of food.</p></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This Ojas of both the Parent get collected in the mother&#8217;s womb for development as Embryo and then into a Life form.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This Ojas of both the Parent can be called the Spiritual Energy also.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The great Tamil Siddhas talk about 15 Amirtha Nilai (Bio Energy or Ojas) in the body, which are nothing but Varma points or Life points.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This Ojas travels from one point to another according to the Tithi or Moon phase, everyday.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The consummation of two different Ojas of Parents on a particular Tithi, results in the formation of Embryo.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The proof of Tithi in menstruation cycle is a well known fact scientifically. This will shake the very foundation of Planets (Grahas) and Nakshatra, as below.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Nakshatra is an Arc of 13 degree 20 minutes of the sidereal zodiac. Each nakshatra has a Lord assigned to it, which is a Graha by Guna.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Each Graha has its Own Guna, which changes according to its placement in a Nakshatra, by the very Owner of the Nakshatra, namely another Graha or itself.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Example : Shani Planet placed in Aswini nakshatra owned by Ketu. So Shani&#8217;s Guna gets modified or affected by Ketu.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In that scenario, predicting based on Shani in this or that house (as asked normally on Quora) becomes baseless. Because Nakshatra division is smaller and more accurate than a house degrees.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">On a side note : In Jaimini System it is most accurate, as the very degree is taken for measurement and predictions. Here Nakshatra position becomes meaningless.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Without knowing the real affectation of a planet in a nakshatra, predictions will be wrong.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Also prediction of a planet in a nakshatra and its events will go wrong as per the timing with Vimshottari Dasha which is based on Chandra only.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Yes a deeper understanding of the fundamentals and connection of nakshatra, its lord, the Graha(s) placed in that nakshatra and how that will extrapolate to the Dasha lord, are the most important ones.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Example : Shani in Aswini nakshatra will NOT be fruitful in Shani or Ketu Dasha/Antara, considering Even the fact that Shani and Ketu go well with each other.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Mar 15, 2021 07:21 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Is Drik Siddhanta or Surya Siddhanta accurate for astrological predictions?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Surya Siddhanta lays down the foundation for Vedic Astrology. This has all the parameters and measurement for making a horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Drik Siddhanta or treatise is the modern version of Surya Siddhanta, wherein the planetary positions are taken from Astronomical data.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So Drik Siddhanta is accurate for horoscope making only.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For definition of the very time in terms of Yugas etc, Surya Siddhanta excels.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Predictions based on a horoscope with Surya or Drik will vary due to different position of Planets (Grahas), due to inaccuracy of Ayanamsa and actual Astronomical position value.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">To get a hold of all the definitions of astrological terms, one should learn from Surya Siddhanta. But for actual making of a horoscope, it is good to use Drik Siddanta and make accurate predictions.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Mar 17, 2021 11:34 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">How do I energize Yantra?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Yantra has the root Yam + Tra, which is Yam is to hold and tra is the instrument.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So a Yantra is nothing but a container or machine which holds.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">A Yantra will contain triangles, squares, circles and other geometrical shapes to contain. Is there some other better alternative?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Hugo or Jekyll are good for static website building.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Other alternatives are there, but the content of your blog should be more textual and not get into HTML-CSS-JS mess.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For example</p><ol><li>Text of your blog can be pure text with formatting with MarkDown. This would help any non-technical person to concentrate more on content writing for the blog than to get into HTML-CSS-JS learning.</li><li>Hugo website creator gives templates to choose for the GUI front-end.</li><li>There is no need for database.</li><li>Google AMP based Hugo templates help in upgrading to the latest technologies.</li><li>There are good webHosts like Netlify to host the Hugo website. Netlify helps in secure, encrypted and domain parking.</li><li>So as a blogger, you write Content in Markdown, push it to Github for storage and maintenance, then use Hugo to push the code to Netlify, to the live website. So simple.</li><li>Hugo is simple and the best.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Addendum : </b><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=0406ee&amp;url=https://stevehora.com" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="stevehora.com"><b>SteveHora.com</b></a></span><b> </b>is build using <b>Markdown, Google AMP, Hugo, Github and Netlify by Steve Hora</b>, himself.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Mar 28, 2021 10:34 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">How does one read Lagna and Navamsa together in a chart?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Lagna chart is D1 and the basic one.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When D1 houses are divided by 9, and the resulting segments or arc are distributed to different houses, one gets Navamsa D9 chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So mathematically as shown in below image.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-b0bbcaaa3df6bfb67879e28c09247fc2" master_src="/img/qimg-b0bbcaaa3df6bfb67879e28c09247fc2" master_w="225" master_h="224" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The angle 30 degrees is divided by 9 to get an Arc of 3 degree 20 minutes, which symbolically belongs to one house or sign.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So logically one part of a house belongs to another part of (same) or another house.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If it is the same, then it becomes vargottama. Like in Mesha Rashi, the first part of D1 or pada (3.333 deg) belongs to Mesha itself as First Navamsa pada and Vargottama.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So a Graha placed in D1 takes another avatar in D9 as per its Sign or House occupation. It does NOT become 30 degrees in that house to claim House lordship, as there are many padas of different D1 houses parts. With this same mathematical analogy, one can prove,that is THERE is NO exaltation or debilitation in any divisional charts.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So one should read the Graha in D1 at house level and at Pada level to that Navamsa Sign.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Mar 29, 2021 12:01 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the significance of Navagraha Shanti Pooja?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">NavaGraha Shanti Pooja is done to appease the Planets or Grahas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This is a astrological remedial procedure at Space (House) and Graha (Energy) level. This does NOT include the Time dimension.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">One can get details from one&#8217;s horoscope, for specificity for a particular graha dosha.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">You can do this puja on your nakshatra day, to remove bad effects of all planets, that way a generic effect can be had.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Mantra, Grain and Color of cloth used in the puja are significant, which the Brahmin or Pujari will take care of.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For example Barley is for Surya, Bengal Gram is for Guru, Toor dhal is for Kuja, Horse gram for Ketu, Green gram is for Budha, Rice with husk is for Chandra, Black sessame seeds for Shani, Uradh dal is for Rahu, White beans is for Shukra.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Read more in the below Q2A,</p><p class="qtext_para"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="/What-are-the-Doshas-in-a-horoscope-and-what-are-the-possible-remedies/answer/Steve-Hora">Steve Hora's answer to What are the Doshas in a horoscope, and what are the possible remedies?</a></span></p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Mar 29, 2021 08:27 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Are all the planets interdependent on each other in some or the other way?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Planets or Grahas are not dependent on each other.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Nor the aspects or drishti gets mixed by combination or whatsoever. This is a fallacy.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The angles or arc define the nature of effect on to a particular house or planet. For example Trine or Squaring.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The effect of drishti or combination changes the bala of that house concerned. Due to which, for a good combination, one finds a greater effect namely raja yoga or otherwise. So there is no transformation of any effect by combination of planets.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The only inter-dependency happens in case of Surya and Chandra with Rahu and Ketu, which is anyway an astronomical phenomenon namely eclipses.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Each aspect of a graha will have an effect in its own time, even if it is combined with some other graha.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Mar 30, 2021 01:43 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Is there a connection between Vedic astrology and the "law of attraction"? How do you manifest your desires?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Yes, there is a connection.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#8220;Yad Bhavam Tad Bhavati&#8221; - What you are is What you become.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-fd8c8b29ee321e8f41e5caf11d128cab" master_src="/img/qimg-fd8c8b29ee321e8f41e5caf11d128cab" master_w="259" master_h="194" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There is a secret time from your horoscope, which is independent of your horoscope itself.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The sidereal zodiac has an Abhijith nakshatra, the 28th nakshatra which is pure and spotless, independent of any horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Same is the case with a born person, who has time period within a lunar month, to manifest his/her thoughts. This is a mathematical time period calculated based on Chandra&#8217;s time period.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The &#8220;Law of Attraction&#8221; is just at the thought level, but Time is the one which allows it to manifest. That time is calculated from the horoscope. And when one thinks of a desire in that time, it manifests. That is the connection with Vedic Astrology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In a way, Hinduism has its Tantric way were a Mantra, Yantra and Tantra is used to manifest one&#8217;s thought desire.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Mar 30, 2021 03:09 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What can Manglik see from Lagna or from the Moon?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Manglik is defined as the position of Kuja or Mars from Lagna, Chandra (Moon) and Shukra (Venus).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The positions is 7th, 8th, 12th, 1st, and 4th, in that order of veeriya.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">12th is for bed pleasures, 1st is for compatibility at mind level, 4th is for happiness, 7th is for married life and 8th is for longevity of married life together.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shukra deals with genes, sperms and ovum. Chandra deals with Manas and Lagna the body. Kuja is Veeriya which can be good or bad.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So accordingly Kuja can affect Mind, Body and Gene propagation in its Veeriya or Strength.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If Kuja is placed in above position, example 7th from Lagna, Chandra and Shukra, it is full manglik.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Apr 01, 2021 09:13 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">If I move somewhere and astrocartography changes my ascendant, should I use the relocated chart to follow my transits?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Your birth horoscope is a snapshot of the zodiac with ascendant at birth, which does not change.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When you move and live somewhere else, then the position of planets and ascendant changes according lat and long of the new place, for the current zodiac which is nothing but Transit.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">AstroCartoGraphy does NOT change your birth chart or its ascendant, which is a given thing by birth to you. Example : Your shape of your nose.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">ACG does change your transit ascendant and planetary position.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When superimposing the current transit over birth chart, one can read the changes including the ascendant.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So ACG cannot be read in isolation. It has to be read with birth chart with its ascendant.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Apr 02, 2021 06:24 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the message of the Tamil song "Enjoy Enjami"?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="/What-is-your-review-of-the-Enjoy-Enjaami-Tamil-song/answer/Steve-Hora">Steve Hora's answer to What is your review of the "Enjoy Enjaami" Tamil song?</a></span></p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Apr 03, 2021 07:30 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Can you do birth time rectification?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Yes, I do birth time certification, but not to a difference of more than <b>&#177;</b> <b>2</b> hours within a house for ascendant.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For people with no TOB, I refer them to Tamil Nadi Palm leaf reading to get an approximate Lagna house.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I use PranaPada Lagna to correct the type of birth, which I had written about in another Q2A.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">With some past life questions and answers, the TOB is made accurate within 1 minute, by correlation with my prediction of life events from the horoscope. The hand is pacifying the land.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The song starts with Parai drums. The Parai is normally drummed in Tamil culture to announce news in a village, arrival of child or death.<br />The song starts with Kulavai or Ulations of women for gathering and celebrations.<br />Here it is used to announce about the start of this song. In a way Parai beating will awaken the Kundalini at the Muladhara chakra, for Energy to surge through the spine. In a death scenario, it is used with Oppari genre, to bring full throttled sadness, to celebrate Death itself and culmination of the Soul. And this is Tamil Culture.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#2965;&#3009;&#2965;&#3021;&#2965;&#3010; &#2965;&#3009;&#2965;&#3021;&#2965;&#3010;<br />Cuckoo is cooing Cuckoo Cuckoo</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#2980;&#3006;&#2980;&#3021;&#2980;&#3006; &#2980;&#3006;&#2980;&#3021;&#2980;&#3006; &#2965;&#2995;&#2997;&#3014;&#2975;&#3021;&#2975;&#3007;<br />Grandpa Grandpa removing the weeds and preparing the soil for sowing.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#2965;&#3009;&#2965;&#3021;&#2965;&#3010; &#2965;&#3009;&#2965;&#3021;&#2965;&#3010;<br />Cuckoo Cuckoo<br />&#2986;&#3018;&#2984;&#3021;&#2980;&#3009;&#2994; &#2991;&#3006;&#2992;&#3009; &#2990;&#3008;&#2985;&#3021; &#2965;&#3018;&#2980;&#3021;&#2980;&#3007;<br />Who is in the Tree-hole Nest, It is the King Fisher</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#2965;&#3009;&#2965;&#3021;&#2965;&#3010; &#2965;&#3009;&#2965;&#3021;&#2965;&#3010;<br />&#2980;&#2979;&#3021;&#2979;&#3007;&#2991;&#3007;&#2994;&#3021; &#2963;&#2975;&#3009;&#2990;&#3021; &#2980;&#2997;&#2995;&#2965;&#3021;&#2965;&#3007;<br />The frog is running in the rain water</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#2965;&#3009;&#2965;&#3021;&#2965;&#3010; &#2965;&#3009;&#2965;&#3021;&#2965;&#3010;<br />&#2965;&#2990;&#3021;&#2986;&#2995;&#3007; &#2986;&#3010;&#2970;&#3021;&#2970;&#3007; &#2980;&#2969;&#3021;&#2965;&#2970;&#3021;&#2970;&#3007;<br />The hairy caterpillar is sister.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It means the King fisher is ready to eat the frog in water, but the frog will not eat the hairy caterpillar, as it is related indirectly to frog. How?. The caterpillar will evolve into an insect which can be eaten by the frog.<br />So natural food chain is told in a Rhyme and Chime of Tamil words called &#2958;&#2980;&#3009;&#2965;&#3016; &#2990;&#3019;&#2985;&#3016;.<br />A lot of Tamil nuances, like this, is there all over the song.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#2949;&#2995;&#3021;&#2995;&#3007; Come together to Enjoy, oh my granddaughter and grandson.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">A beautiful musical-drama between grandma and grandson conversation, set in rural scenario, with the theme of Nature and Forefather&#8217;s way of living and their appreciation, knowledge and understanding of Nature, blended with their language and culture. Tithi is every 12 degrees angular difference between Sun &amp; Moon. The formula to calculate is (Moon &#8211; Sun Long)/12 = Tithi number.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Vara</b>: Vara is a week day based on the ruler namely Sun, Moon, Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus and Saturn. Vara does not have a mathematical Start, but the sequence has.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Nakshatra</b>: The zodiac is divided into the 360 degrees which is in turn divided into 27 Nakshatras. The &#8220;Start of Aries&#8221; defines the start of the first Nakshatra namely Aswini. But the very start of Aries, depends on Ayanamsa, which is controversial and mathematically differs, due to an astronomical fact namely coincidence of Sidereal and Tropical zodiac.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Yoga</b>: Yoga is calculated by adding the longitudes of Sun and moon and dividing it into 27 equal parts. The longitudes of Sun and Moon in sidereal calculations, depends on Ayanamsa, which again varies with different values of it.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Karana: A Karana is half of the Tithi, so dependent for its value on its primary value of Tithi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Tithi is the angular distance between Sun and Moon AND REMAINS the SAME, whether it is Sidereal or Tropical zodiac and INDEPENDENT of Ayanamsa, calculations.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So Tithi calculation and observance is the Most accurate and best for any Muhurtha or Horoscopes.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Apr 11, 2021 06:40 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the prediction for Saptami (7th) Tithi born person as per Rishi Agasthiya?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Saptami </b>Tithi is the <b>7th </b>Tithi after Pournima (Full Moon) or Amavasya (New Moon).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The person born in this tithi, is Strong and Fearless and Valiant. This makes the 10th house and its occupants very very significant.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">That is why the whole of human race and other species, work and work and try to accrue more from the 10th house, which is profession, social status and survival.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So it becomes trivial and fundamental to read Kendra houses to know the most fundamental aspects of a person&#8217;s horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Like this one has to understand and then apply the theoretical information to practical use.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For Example : In my chart, Lagna Makara Shani is in 1st house. A Panapara is kind of guarantee or promise in the future.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">9th is also a Apoklima house. Apoklima indicates weakness and becoming less.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">1st house being pure Kona and as well Kendra, becomes first class beneficent.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The grahas occupying a Kona house, shows its significance according to its Guna from the horoscope, good or bad.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Like this one has to understand and then apply the theoretical information to practical use.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For Example : In my chart, Lagna Makara Shani is in 1st house. Makes this Kona and Kendra house most auspicious and powerful.<br />My 5th house has Kendra lord Chandra, making it strong and auspicious.<br />My 9th house is vacant but looked by its own lord Budha, It will be 2.</li><li>Add this number to multiples of 12.</li><li>It will be 12+2 = 14, 26, 38, 50 and so on.</li><li>These years will be significant for the houses concerned.</li></ol><p Moon should be vacant so that this Yoga can be formed.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It is also formed when the Moon is not aspect by an auspicious planet or is not in association with an auspicious planet. Rahu and Ketu are not analyzed when we talk about Kemadruma Yoga.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There is a misconception about Kemadruma yoga that it provides a person with a troubled life. Hence, many astrologers believe this yoga to be inauspicious.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Answer<br /></b>Shastras explain a particular chart. They do NOT lay down proper rules for any yoga.<br />It is a observed fact NOT a true fact.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Each chart is unique with its own ascendant which is again unique.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Kemadruma is from Chandra, which is second to the first, which is ascendant based.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr called auspicious planets can become evil.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So the definition is self defeating.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Mixing mundane 6th and 8th from Chandra for Grahas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Take the ascendant and classify the grahas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Then read the chart, for Poverty which is Kemadruma.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Adhi Yoga</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If not the position of Grahas from Chandra Navamsa?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Moon or Chandra is the signifier of the Mind and gives Mental ability to a person.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Moon is also the nearest satellite or Graha to Earth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Being a Graha which means Pulls or Effects, Moon plays an important role in many of the natural cycles of weather, ovulation, and lunar affectations.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In Vedic Astrology, prime importance is given to it, with equal importance to Sun and Ascendant.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If Sun is Father, Moon is Mother in mundane interpretations of Vedic Astrology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As Moon travels the sky it goes to different Rashis or Moon Signs. Each Sign has been assigned to different planets or Graha, which changes the affectation of the Moon accordingly. Accordingly the significance.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If say Moon is in Vrishabha or Taurus, it will be influenced by Shukra or Venus at the sign level.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">With finer divisions of Nakshatra, which define the karmic aspect of one&#8217;s life, the Nakshatra Lord plays an important role at that level.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If say Chandra is in Krithika Nakshatra of Vrishabha Rashi, then Surya or Sun will have its impact on this person at this level.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Rashis are divided into nine equal parts of Navamsa pada and get distributed to all the signs, then Chandra gets a different power or significance.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If say Chandra is in Krithika Pada 3, then it goes into Kumbha or Aquarius Navamsa, which makes Moon get Shani&#8217;s significance to it.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-ea37215fba39495dfed599e7375f37e4" master_src="/img/qimg-ea37215fba39495dfed599e7375f37e4" master_w="300" master_h="168" /></div></div></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Sep 23, 2021 03:16 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the significance of a planet, its placement in a Rashi, in a Nakshatra, and in a Navamsa?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-7929316dea8d6c7c47f849310a7b5ae8" master_src="/img/qimg-7929316dea8d6c7c47f849310a7b5ae8" master_w="600" master_h="560" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Graha means Pulls or Effects. divisional chart?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Let us take today&#8217;s chart (31st Oct 2021).</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="portrait qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-021b1ecc8b4a0e60a13c7b850a10be19" u-ltr u-text-align--start">In Vimsamsa (D-20), for example, you find Rahu-Ketu &#8216;conjunct&#8217; in Vrishabha Rashi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Does that mean the consider there are two parallel roads running between two places, and two cars on each road, traveling and at the same place in between. It means they are running parallel separated by a distance but in the same sign or place or range.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So only a significance can be attached to Rahu or Ketu separately, that being, affecting that sign, not &#8216;conjunctly&#8217;. Period.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There goes down much fallacy of divisional charts, read as in D-1 or yogas in it and &#8216;conjunct&#8217; theories.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Oct 30, 2021 06:14 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What does Rahu Ketu conjunction mean in divisional charts? astrological texts should be read, understood, and then applied to a horoscope.</p><ol><li>The yoga forming Graha(s) should be analyzed for its position, strength, and its Drishti.</li><li>To which houses this yoga pertains also should be taken into account.<br />Example: If it is Dhana yoga, then it pertains to 2nd, 11th, and 9th.</li><li>What this grahas and houses signify for this yoga has to it is a positional shift, which is just Energy and Space, NOT Time.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So Neecha Banga is yoga that can happen anytime or ever-present. As in the case of Master Batsman Sachin Tendulkar.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-b456bdd652965c16ee7cc0aaddb406d8" master_src="/img/qimg-b456bdd652965c16ee7cc0aaddb406d8" master_w="463" master_h="233" /></div></div></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Nov 18, 2021 07:10 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the Shani planet and its significance?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Shani or Saturn </b>is one of the farthest planets or Graha of our Solar system.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Due to which it is cold, isolated, and just the opposite of Surya or Sun which is hot.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So significance at a metaphysical level in Vedic astrology with lonely, cold in behavior and not conducive for life.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shani takes roughly 30 solar years to go around the Sun, and by observation, patterns and behaviors in a person&#8217;s life as seen from the horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The patterns were repetitive and so a karmic significance is attached to Shani, and that was extrapolated between births.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In a way, Shani takes care of the Karmic cycle of birth, death, Karma as Punya and Papa.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shani is inimical to Surya, but Surya is not. This is explained by the story of Shani as the stepson of Surya, born to Chaya (Shade) of Sun.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Due to this Shani hates Surya, but Surya bestows good vibes towards Shani as a father.</p><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">He represents <b>longevity, determination, losses, accidents renunciation</b>, prosperity, lunacy, servants, and death in a horoscope. He also represents oil, black color, disease, lunacy, toddy sellers, iron merchants, thieves, litigations, and jailhouses.</p></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">By observation, Shani had been given the above significance, based on many horoscopes, which can be debated also.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shani rules Makara and Kumbha, exalted in Thula and debilitated in Mesha.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shani does not like hot planets, especially Mars or Kuja.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In Makara of Shani&#8217;s house, Kuja is exalted but debilitated in Mesha of Kuja house.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So Shani&#8217;s arch-enemy is Kuja, due to the above disrespect of Kuja.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shani is more powerful than any other planet including Guru or Jupiter. But less powerful than Surya.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In a horoscope, if Shani is well placed, he bestows riches and fame.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Example</b><br />Shani is in his own house Makara with friend Ketu, and in Lagna, for me. He bestowed me with gnana and karmic yoga to my mind or brain, to find the truth behind this karmic subject namely Vedic Astrology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So be it. How does it work?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><ul><li>Prasna or Horary Astrology is one of the six branches of Vedic Astrology.</li></ul><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Other branches namely are</p><ul><li>Kundali or Jathakam or Natal Astrology,</li><li>Muhurta or Electional astrology</li><li>Nimitta or Omen interpretation,</li><li>Gola or Astronomical study.</li><li>Ganita or Astronomical math.</li></ul><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-a735cf6f92caed8ab91fd7eb4c37bf76" master_src="/img/qimg-a735cf6f92caed8ab91fd7eb4c37bf76" master_w="277" master_h="182" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ashtamangala Prasna is practiced widely in Kerala.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It uses 108 cowries or shells to predict the Past, Present, and Future of the question or Prashan asked.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The cowries are divided randomly into three parts or piles.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Each pile is counted off as multiples of 8 and the remainder is taken.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If the remainder is zero, 8 cowries are taken.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The 3 remainders from Left to Right, are the Past, Present, and Future of the question asked.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Odd numbers are good, even numbers are bad.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">A horoscope is made for the exact time of the question as asked by the questioner and predictions made based on the house to which question pertains, lord, Grahas, and Drishtis on that house, ruling nakshatra, etc.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Prasna Marga is good in itself and divine and NOT a replacement of Kundali, which is based on the karma of the person.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Without a good Astrological Guru and Guru Dakshina, Prasna will not be fruitful.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So be it, Tathaastu.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 21, 2022 09:49 PM PST</span></div></p><hr But does not connect it with Navamsa or Vimshottari.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Later modern authors had connected Tara and Vimshotari together for ascertaining the good or bad effects of different Dashas based on nav-tara. It is possible, but this in itself per se Does NOT help in predicting an event. The reasons are many, namely,</p><ul><li>The nakshatra is NOT the house lord or the Graha itself, directly.</li><li>The Tara sequence is numerical, but not the time in Vimshottari.</li><li>Based on only Chandra, is not fully qualified, as Chandra is itself is a Graha.</li></ul><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So Tara Chakra can give an indication, but cannot decide or delineate the time for the event.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As such Tara Chakra is effective in transit, horary, and mundane predictions.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Navamsa is more connected to Rashi or Lagna chart to delineate the karma of each house or Graha.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Nakshatra is the key to the timing of events.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The key secret is how one connects a Graha, Nakshatra Lord, and House lord with Vimshottari Dasha Lord, for prediction of events.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Feb 05, 2022 09:16 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What More on it now.<br />Navamsa is used to get that particular Palm Leaf bundle based on a person&#8217;s unique fingerprint.<br />The Tamil alphabets are as below. <br />12 - Uyir (Life) as in Tamil or vowels.<br />18 - Mei (Body) or consonants.<br />Combining above Life and Body gives Uyir-Mei (Life-Body) which gives a Soul a Name.<br />So 12 * 18 = 216, which is twice the magic Hindu number 108 and the total Navamsa padas. <br />Below are the letters. <br />216 + 12 + 18 = 246 with a support letter which is "Akk" used to form the base of Mai letters, which can be ignored as no words are formed with it as a starting letter.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Simply put, in Tamil, no words can start with, for example, "ik", "ich"and so on. The last column in the below table.<br />So there can only 228 legal letters that can be used for a Name.<br />So there are only 216+12, which can be distributed to each navamsa pada and 12 Rashi's used for names. <br />For example, "Cha" or &#2970; is assigned to Navamsa pada in Vrishabha Rashi. <br />In a sequential way, all the Uyir and Uyir-Mei letters are distributed to All navamsas and Rashis.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Tamil grammar disallows 108 letters as first letter of a word or name. The disallowed letters are &#2969;, &#2975;	&#2979;, &#2992;, &#2994;, &#2996;, &#2995;, &#2993;, &#2985; and its Uyir-Mei derivatives, which amounts to 9 * 12 = 108.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Removing them from below list, the left over is just 108 to be assigned to all Navamsa padas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As the Tamil language was founded by Sage Agastiya, who also wrote most of the "Tamil Palm Leaf Astrological Reading", this codification was followed by him.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">With his profound extra-perceptional mind, he moved from one Nadi to another in time, to write down the fate or destiny of to be born persons.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But there can be thousands of people born in each Nadi, with the same letter starting. Taking that into account, there are 150 nadis in a Rashi and a Rashi consists of 9 navamsa padas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Extrapolating one can only map the first letter and sound from the Rashi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In a Palm leaf reading, one can ascertain mathematically the first letter and consequent letters of oneself, father&#8217;s and mother&#8217;s name. Thus the name was found.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-b41113eef8d88203f5f9fc155fd18596" master_src="/img/qimg-b41113eef8d88203f5f9fc155fd18596" master_w="602" master_h="380" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="/What-are-the-secrets-behind-the-Navamsa-chart-in-connection-with-Nadi-palm-leaf-reading/answer/Steve-Hora">Steve Hora's answer to What are the secrets behind the Navamsa chart in connection with Nadi palm leaf reading?</a></span></p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Aug 25, 2022 07:36 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is Nadi Amsa? of each Rashi in Lagna chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Nadis are unequal divisions according to 16 Shodhasa Varga chart divisions.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For Fixed signs it is in reverse order 150 to 1.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For Dual signs it starts from the middle 76th division as 1 and resets as 76 from start.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The names are as below for all above types of signs.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Vasudhaa, Vaishnavi, Braahmi, Kaalakoota, Shaankari, Sudhaakari, Samaa, Saumyaa, Suraa, Maayaa, Manoharaa, Maadhavi, Manjuswanaa, Ghoraa, Kumbhini, Kutilaa, Prabhaa, Paraa, Payasvini, Maalaa, Jagati, Jarjharaa, Dhruvaa, Musalaa, Mudgaraa, Paashaa, Champakaa, Daamakaa(Daamini), Mahi, Kulashaa, Kamalaa, Kaantaa, Kaalaa, Karikaraa, Kahamaa, Durdharaa, Durbhagaa, Vishwaa, Visheernaa, Vikataa, Avilaa, Vibhramaa, Sukhadaa, Snigdhaa, Sodaraa, Surasundari, Amritaplaavini, Kaalaa, Kaamadhuk, Karaveerani, Gahvaraa, Kundini, Raudraa, Vishaakhyaa, Vishanaashini, Narmadaa, Sheetalaa, Nimnaa, Preetaa, Priyavardhini, Maanaghnaa, Durbhagaa, Chiraa, Chitrini, Chiranjeevini, Bhoopaa, Gakaharaa, Naalaa, Nalini, Nirmalaa, Nadi, Sudhaamritaamshu, Kaalikaa, Kalushankuraa, Trailokyamohankari, Mahaamaari, Susheetalaa, Sukhadaa, Suprabhaa, Shobhaa, Shobhanaa, Shivadaa, Shivaa, Balaa, Jwaalaa, Gadaa, Gaadhaa, Nootanaa, Sumanoharaa, Somavalli, Somalataa, Mangalaa, Mudrikaa, Kshudhaa, Mokshaapavargaa, Balayaa, Navaneeta, Nishaachari, Nirritti, Nigadaa, Saraa, Sangeetaa, Saamadaa, Samaa, Viwhwambharaa, Kumaari, Kokilaa, Kunjaraakriti, Aindraa, Swaahaa, Swaraa, Vahni, Preetaa, Rakshajalaaplavaa, Vaaruni, Madiraa, Maitri, Haarini, Harini, Marut, Dhananjayaa, Dhanakari, Dhanadaa, Kamchhapaambuja, Maamshaani, Shooeini, Raudri, Shivaa, Shivakari, Kalaa, Kundaa, Mukundaa, Bharataa, Haritaa, Kadalee, Smaraa, Kandalaa, Kokilaa, Paapaa, Kaamini, Kalashodbhavaa, Veeraprasoo, Sangaraa, Shatayajnaa, Shataavari, Prahvi, Paatalini, Naagaa, Pankajaa and Parameshwari.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Jagannatha Hora software gives the Index, Division and Name for each of the Grahas and Lagna of a Lagna chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Lagna in Lagna chart and NadiAmsa lagna placement are the most important for general predictions called as General Chapter reading or "Pothu Kandam" as in Tamil Palm Leaf astrological reading.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The other grahas as per their house lordship and its significance are read from that Graha position and its NadiAmsa position.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For example 10th house is for Career, and if its house lord in Shukra, then its position in Lagna and NadiAmsa chart becomes "Thozhil Kandam" as in Tamil.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In a practical chart, Guru was 9th lord placed was well in 1st house of Mesha, but the Nadi of Guru was in Kataka, which is 8th from 9th. So in the Mahadasa of Guru and Antara of Chandra (placed in 7th Thula), the person lost her father.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So one can read from Tamil Palm leaf, their Life readings, which are costly. Or.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Mathematically calculate as above and get life predictions.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-bc658cb4e7e1ced4e675e17e3e931fd3" master_src="/img/qimg-bc658cb4e7e1ced4e675e17e3e931fd3" master_w="309" master_h="163" /></div></div></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Aug 27, 2022 09:43 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /></div>
